24/07/23, 1:12â€¯am - +91 97675 85518: *Important post regarding temporary accommodation*

Hello guys,
I have been getting a lot of messages regarding availability of temporary accommodation, and it seems to be the case that not enough temporary accommodations are available. The temporary accommodations in West Hall I believe are filling fast or might be full. Also, there is limited availability in Airbnb's nearby Arlington, and even though some might be available, they are way too expensive for an international student. With the number of incoming students in the Fall semester being high as always, people are having a very tough time finding temporary accommodation.

Now adding to this, current students who are having their lease until 31st July, and are starting a new lease(somewhere around mid August) are also finding it tough to find temporary accommodation. Some of these students are currently enrolled in in-person summer courses, and commuting from an Airbnb or motel to lectures is not an economical viable option.

So, temporary accommodation seems to be a common issue for incoming as well as current students. To try to resolve this issue, I am circulating a Google Form, where anyone who needs a temporary accommodation can fill their details(Name, Student ID, Start Date, End Date). I am planning to send the list of names to the university, so that they might make some arrangements during such a critical period. I know that this might prove to be worthless, and the university might not care, but its still worth a try. I had already tried this back in 2021, but they didnt seem to care, maybe this time they will.

*Important note for recently graduated students*: People who have graduated right now and need temporary accommodation, please do not fill this form as the university will not entertain any requests for already graduated students.

Please feel free to post your comments and suggestions regarding the same.

Thank you.

27/07/23, 2:10â€¯am - +91 97675 85518: *Important post regarding temporary accommodation*

Hello guys,
I have been getting a lot of messages regarding availability of temporary accommodation, and it seems to be the case that not enough temporary accommodations are available. The temporary accommodations in West Hall I believe are filling fast or might be full. Also, there is limited availability in Airbnb's nearby Arlington, and even though some might be available, they are way too expensive for an international student. With the number of incoming students in the Fall semester being high as always, people are having a very tough time finding temporary accommodation.

Now adding to this, current students who are having their lease until 31st July, and are starting a new lease(somewhere around mid August) are also finding it tough to find temporary accommodation. Some of these students are currently enrolled in in-person summer courses, and commuting from an Airbnb or motel to lectures is not an economical viable option.

So, temporary accommodation seems to be a common issue for incoming as well as current students. To try to resolve this issue, I am circulating a Google Form, where anyone who needs a temporary accommodation can fill their details(Name, Student ID, Start Date, End Date). I am planning to send the list of names to the university, so that they might make some arrangements during such a critical period. I know that this might prove to be worthless, and the university might not care, but its still worth a try. I had already tried this back in 2021, but they didnt seem to care, maybe this time they will.

*Important note for recently graduated students*: People who have graduated right now and need temporary accommodation, please do not fill this form as the university will not entertain any requests for already graduated students.

Please feel free to post your comments and suggestions regarding the same.

Thank you.
